Remains to prove termination of a 40-rules system (40 strict rules).

Remains to prove termination of a 39-rules system (39 strict rules).

Remains to prove termination of a 141-rules system (102 strict rules).

Remains to prove termination of a 1147-rules system (140 strict rules).
